# End-to-End: How Kubernetes Creates a Deployment

## Your Task

You are onboarding to the Kubernetes project. A senior engineer has asked you to produce
a technical explanation of how a Kubernetes Deployment gets created — tracing the full
request flow from a client application through the API server and into persistent storage.

**Your question**: Explain how a Kubernetes client application creates a Deployment from
start to finish. Your explanation must trace through all three layers:

1. **Client library** — What type/function in `kubernetes-client-go` sends the HTTP request?
2. **API server** — What function in `kubernetes/kubernetes` receives and validates the create request?
3. **Storage** — What function in `etcd-io/etcd` persists the Deployment to the key-value store?

For each step, cite the specific repository, file path, and function/type name.

## Context

You are working in a Kubernetes ecosystem with the following repos:

- `kubernetes/kubernetes` (the core orchestrator)
- `sg-evals/kubernetes-client-go` (go-client-library)
- `sg-evals/kubernetes-api` (api-type-definitions)
- `etcd-io/etcd` (distributed-kv-store)

This question is specifically designed to benefit from cross-repo synthesis. Use your
search tools to trace the full path across repositories.

## Output Format

Create a file at `/workspace/answer.json` with your findings:

```json
{
  "chain": [
    {
      "repo": "sg-evals/kubernetes-client-go",
      "path": "relative/path/to/file.go",
      "symbol": "FunctionOrTypeName",
      "description": "What this step does in the flow"
    }
  ],
  "text": "Comprehensive narrative explaining the end-to-end flow, citing specific files and functions from each repo."
}
```

**Important**: Use the exact repo identifiers specified for this task. The oracle expects `repo` values of `sg-evals/kubernetes-client-go` (client layer), `kubernetes/kubernetes` (API server layer), and `etcd-io/etcd` (storage layer). The `repo` field must match these exactly.
**Note**: Tool output may return repo names with a `github.com/` prefix (e.g., `github.com/sg-evals/kubernetes-client-go`). Strip this prefix in your answer — use `sg-evals/kubernetes-client-go`, NOT `github.com/sg-evals/kubernetes-client-go`.

The `chain` should contain at least 3 steps representing the 3 layers described above.

## Evaluation

Your answer will be scored on:
- **Flow coverage**: Does the chain include key steps from all 3 layers (client → server → storage)?
- **Technical accuracy**: Are the cited file paths and function names correct?
- **Provenance**: Does your narrative reference all three repositories?
- **Synthesis quality** (supplementary): Does the explanation connect the layers clearly?


   - `Deployments(namespace)` method (line 51-53 in `apps_client.go`) returns a `DeploymentInterface`

2. **DeploymentInterface is implemented by the `deployments` struct** (lines 65-68 in `deployment.go`)

3. **The actual HTTP request is sent by**: The `Client[T].Create()` method
   - **File**: `/workspace/client-go/gentype/type.go`
   - **Function**: `Client[T].Create()` (lines 243-255)

### The HTTP Request Implementation

The actual function that sends the HTTP POST request is in `/workspace/client-go/gentype/type.go`, lines 243-255:

```go
func (c *Client[T]) Create(ctx context.Context, obj T, opts metav1.CreateOptions) (T, error) {
	result := c.newObject()
	err := c.client.Post().
		UseProtobufAsDefaultIfPreferred(c.prefersProtobuf).
		NamespaceIfScoped(c.namespace, c.namespace != "").
		Resource(c.resource).
		VersionedParams(&opts, c.parameterCodec).
		Body(obj).
		Do(ctx).
		Into(result)
	return result, err
}
```

- Calls `c.client.Post()` on the REST client
- Adds the namespace and resource ("deployments")
- Sets the request

   266→// NamespaceKeyRootFunc is the default function for constructing storage paths
   267→// to resource directories enforcing namespace rules.
   268→func NamespaceKeyRootFunc(ctx context.Context, prefix string) string {
   269→	key := prefix
   270→	ns, ok := genericapirequest.NamespaceFrom(ctx)
   271→	if ok && len(ns) > 0 {
   272→		key = key + "/" + ns
   273→	}
   274→	return key
   275→}
   276→
   277→// NamespaceKeyFunc is the default function for constructing storage paths to
   278→// a resource relative to the given prefix enforcing namespace rules. If the
   279→// context does not contain a namespace, it errors.

   560→// ShouldDeleteDuringUpdate is the default function for

   562→// It checks if the new object has no finalizers,
   563→// the existing object's deletionTimestamp is set, and
   564→// the existing object's deletionGracePeriodSeconds is 0 or nil

147-assistanttext-
Perfect! I've successfully traced the complete end-to-end flow of how a Kubernetes Deployment gets created across all three layers. Here's a summary of what I found:

## Key Findings

**Client Layer** (`sg-evals/kubernetes-client-go`):
- **Entry point**: `DeploymentInterface.Create()` in `kubernetes/typed/apps/v1/deployment.go`
- **HTTP sender**: `Client[T].Create()` in `gentype/type.go` (lines 244-255)
- Serializes the Deployment and sends a POST request

**API Server Layer** (`kubernetes/kubernetes`):
- **Request handler**: `createHandler()` in `staging/src/k8s.io/apiserver/pkg/endpoints/handlers/create.go` (lines 53-236)
- **Storage orchestrator**: `Store.Create()` and internal `create()` in `staging/src/k8s.io/apiserver/pkg/registry/generic/registry/store.go`
- **Validation**: `DeploymentStrategy.PrepareForCreate()` in `pkg/registry/apps/deployment/strategy.go`
- Validates the object, runs admission webhooks, and prepares for storage

**Storage Layer** (`etcd-io/etcd`):
- **RPC handler**: `applierV3backend.Put()` in `server/etcdserver/apply.go` (lines 249-303)
- **MVCC persistence**: `storeTxnWrite.Put/put()` in `server/mvcc/kvstore_txn.go` (lines 109-253)
  - Creates an `mvccpb.KeyValue` protobuf with the Deployment data
- **Backend storage**: `batchTx.unsafePut()` in `server/mvcc/backend/batch_tx.go` (lines 149-171)
  - Persists to BoltDB's memory-mapped B+ tree

The complete answer with citations, file paths, and a detailed narrative has been saved to `/workspace/answer.json`.

probability of any generated name conflicting with existing names.\n   437\u2192// Without retry, a 0.1% probability occurs at ~500\n   438\u2192// generated names and a 50% probability occurs at ~4500\n   439\u2192// generated names.\n   440\u2192const maxNameGenerationCreateAttempts = 8\n   441\u2192\n   442\u2192// Create inserts a new item according to the unique key from the object.\n   443\u2192// Note that registries may mutate the input object (e.g. in the strategy\n   444\u2192// hooks). trace, nil\n   303\u2192}\n   304\u2192\n   305\u2192func (a *applierV3backend) DeleteRange(txn mvcc.TxnWrite, dr *pb.DeleteRangeRequest) (*pb.DeleteRangeResponse, error) {\n   306\u2192\tresp := && sortOrder == pb.RangeRequest_NONE {\n   385\u2192\t\t// Since current mvcc.Range implementation returns results\n   386\u2192\t\t// sorted by keys in lexiographically ascending order,\n   387\u2192\t\t// sort ASCEND by default only when target is not 'KEY'\n   388\u2192\t\tsortOrder = pb.RangeRequest_ASCEND\n   389\u2192\t}\n   390\u2192\tif sortOrder != pb.RangeRequest_NONE {\n   391\u2192\t\tvar sorter sort.Interface\n   392\u2192\t\tswitch {\n   393\u2192\t\tcase r.SortTarget == pb.RangeRequest_KEY:\n   394\u2192\t\t\tsorter = &kvSortByKey{&kvSort{rr.KVs}}\n   395\u2192\t\tcase r.SortTarget == pb.RangeRequest_VERSION:\n   396\u2192\t\t\tsorter = &kvSortByVersion{&kvSort{rr.KVs}}\n   397\u2192\t\tcase r.SortTarget == pb.RangeRequest_CREATE:\n   398\u2192\t\t\tsorter = &kvSortByCreate{&kvSort{rr.KVs}}\n   399\u2192\t\tcase r.SortTarget == pb.RangeRequest_MOD:\n   400\u2192\t\t\tsorter = &kvSortByMod{&kvSort{rr.KVs}}\n   401\u2192\t\tcase 410\u2192\t}\n   411\u2192\n   412\u2192\tif r.Limit > 0 && len(rr.KVs) > int(r.Limit) {\n   413\u2192\t\trr.KVs = rr.KVs[:r.Limit]\n   414\u2192\t\tresp.More = true\n   415\u2192\t}\n   416\u2192\ttrace.Step(\"filter and sort the key-value pairs\")\n   417\u2192\tresp.Header.Revision = rr.Rev\n   418\u2192\tresp.Count = int64(rr.Count)\n   419\u2192\tresp.Kvs = &rr.KVs[i]\n   425\u2192\t}\n   426\u2192\ttrace.Step(\"assemble the response\")\n   427\u2192\treturn resp, nil\n   428\u2192}\n   429\u2192\n   430\u2192func (a *applierV3backend) Txn(ctx context.Context, rt *pb.TxnRequest) (*pb.TxnResponse, *traceutil.Trace, error) {\n   431\u2192\tlg := a.s.Logger()\n   432\u2192\ttrace := traceutil.Get(ctx)\n   433\u2192\tif trace.IsEmpty() {\n   434\u2192\t\ttrace = traceutil.New(\"transaction\", a.s.Logger())\n   435\u2192\t\tctx = context.WithValue(ctx, traceutil.TraceKey, trace)\n   436\u2192\t}\n   437\u2192\tisWrite := !isTxnReadonly(rt)\n   438\u2192\n   439\u2192\t// When the transaction contains write operations, we use ReadTx instead of\n   440\u2192\t// ConcurrentReadTx to avoid extra overhead of copying buffer.\n   441\u2192\tvar txn mvcc.TxnWrite\n   442\u2192\tif isWrite && a.s.Cfg.ExperimentalTxnModeWriteWithSharedBuffer {\n   443\u2192\t\ttxn = mvcc.NewReadOnlyTxnWrite(a.s.KV().Read(mvcc.SharedBufReadTxMode, trace))\n   444\u2192\t} else {\n   445\u2192\t\ttxn = mvcc.NewReadOnlyTxnWrite(a.s.KV().Read(mvcc.ConcurrentReadTxMode, trace))\n   446\u2192\t}\n   447\u2192\n   448\u2192\tvar txnPath []bool\n   449\u2192\ttrace.StepWithFunction(\n   450\u2192\t\tfunc() {\n   451\u2192\t\t\ttxnPath = compareToPath(txn, rt)\n   452\u2192\t\t},\n   453\u2192\t\t\"compare\",\n   454\u2192\t)\n   455\u2192\n   456\u2192\tif isWrite {\n   457\u2192\t\ttrace.AddField(traceutil.Field{Key: \"read_only\", Value: false})\n   458\u2192\t\tif _, err := checkRequests(txn, rt, txnPath, a.checkPut); err != nil {\n   459\u2192\t\t\ttxn.End()\n   460\u2192\t\t\treturn nil, nil, err\n   461\u2192\t\t}\n   462\u2192\t}\n   463\u2192\tif _, err := checkRequests(txn, rt, txnPath, a.checkRange); err != nil {\n   464\u2192\t\ttxn.End()\n   465\u2192\t\treturn nil, nil, err\n   466\u2192\t}\n   467\u2192\ttrace.Step(\"check requests\")\n   468\u2192\ttxnResp, _ := newTxnResp(rt, txnPath)\n   469\u2192\n   470\u2192\t// When executing mutable txn ops, etcd must hold the txn lock so\n   471\u2192\t// readers do not see any intermediate results. Since writes are\n   472\u2192\t// serialized on the raft loop, the revision in the read view will\n   473\u2192\t// be the revision of the write txn.\n   474\u2192\tif isWrite {\n   475\u2192\t\ttxn.End()\n   476\u2192\t\ttxn = a.s.KV().Write(trace)\n   477\u2192\t}\n   478\u2192\t_, err := a.applyTxn(ctx, txn, rt, txnPath, txnResp)\n   479\u2192\tif err != nil {\n   480\u2192\t\tif isWrite {\n   481\u2192\t\t\t// CAUTION: When a txn performing write operations starts, we always expect it to be successful.\n   482\u2192\t\t\t// If a write failure is seen we SHOULD NOT try to recover the server, but crash with a panic to make the failure explicit.\n   483\u2192\t\t\t// Trying to silently recover (e.g by ignoring the failed txn or calling txn.End() early) poses serious risks:\n   484\u2192\t\t\t// - violation of transaction atomicity if some write operations have been partially executed\n   485\u2192\t\t\t// - data inconsistency across different etcd members if they applied the txn asymmetrically\n   486\u2192\t\t\tlg.Panic(\"unexpected error during txn with writes\", zap.Error(err))\n   487\u2192\t\t} else {\n   488\u2192\t\t\tlg.Error(\"unexpected error during readonly txn\", zap.Error(err))\n   489\u2192\t\t}\n   490\u2192\t}\n   491\u2192\trev := txn.Rev()\n   492\u2192\tif len(txn.Changes()) != 0 {\n   493\u2192\t\trev++\n   494\u2192\t}\n   495\u2192\ttxn.End()\n   496\u2192\n   497\u2192\ttxnResp.Header.Revision = rev\n   498\u2192\ttrace.AddField(\n   499\u2192\t\ttraceutil.Field{Key: \"number_of_response\", Value: len(txnResp.Responses)},\n   500\u2192\t\ttraceutil.Field{Key: \"response_revision\", Value: txnResp.Header.Revision},\n   501\u2192\t)\n   502\u2192\treturn txnResp, trace, err\n   503\u2192}\n   504\u2192\n   505\u2192// newTxnResp allocates a txn response for a txn request given a path.\n   506\u2192func newTxnResp(rt *pb.TxnRequest, txnPath []bool) (txnResp *pb.TxnResponse, txnCount int) {\n   507\u2192\treqs := rt.Success\n   508\u2192\tif !txnPath[0] {\n   509\u2192\t\treqs = rt.Failure\n   510\u2192\t}\n   511\u2192\tresps := make([]*pb.ResponseOp, len(reqs))\n   512\u2192\ttxnResp = &pb.TxnResponse{\n   513\u2192\t\tResponses: resps,\n   514\u2192\t\tSucceeded: txnPath[0],\n   515\u2192\t\tHeader:    &pb.ResponseHeader{},\n   516\u2192\t}\n   517\u2192\tfor i, req := range reqs {\n   518\u2192\t\tswitch tv := req.Request.(type) {\n   519\u2192\t\tcase *pb.RequestOp_RequestRange:\n   520\u2192\t\t\tresps[i] = &pb.ResponseOp{Response: &pb.ResponseOp_ResponseRange{}}\n   521\u2192\t\tcase *pb.RequestOp_RequestPut:\n   522\u2192\t\t\tresps[i] = &pb.ResponseOp{Response: &pb.ResponseOp_ResponsePut{}}\n   523\u2192\t\tcase *pb.RequestOp_RequestDeleteRange:\n   524\u2192\t\t\tresps[i] = &pb.ResponseOp{Response: &pb.ResponseOp_ResponseDeleteRange{}}\n   525\u2192\t\tcase *pb.RequestOp_RequestTxn:\n   526\u2192\t\t\tresp, txns := newTxnResp(tv.RequestTxn, txnPath[1:])\n   527\u2192\t\t\tresps[i] = &pb.ResponseOp{Response: &pb.ResponseOp_ResponseTxn{ResponseTxn: resp}}\n   528\u2192\t\t\ttxnPath = txnPath[1+txns:]\n   529\u2192\t\t\ttxnCount += txns + 1\n   530\u2192\t\tdefault:\n   531\u2192\t\t}\n   532\u2192\t}\n   533\u2192\treturn txnResp, txnCount\n   534\u2192}\n   535\u2192\n   536\u2192func compareToPath(rv mvcc.ReadView, rt *pb.TxnRequest) []bool {\n   537\u2192\ttxnPath := make([]bool, 1)\n   538\u2192\tops := rt.Success\n   539\u2192\tif txnPath[0] = applyCompares(rv, rt.Compare); !txnPath[0] {\n   540\u2192\t\tops = rt.Failure\n   541\u2192\t}\n   542\u2192\tfor _, op := range ops {\n   543\u2192\t\ttv, ok := op.Request.(*pb.RequestOp_RequestTxn)\n   544\u2192\t\tif !ok || tv.RequestTxn == nil {\n   545\u2192\t\t\tcontinue\n   546\u2192\t\t}\n   547\u2192\t\ttxnPath = append(txnPath, compareToPath(rv, tv.RequestTxn)...)\n   548\u2192\t}\n   549\u2192\treturn txnPath\n   550\u2192}\n   551\u2192\n   552\u2192func applyCompares(rv mvcc.ReadView, cmps []*pb.Compare) bool {\n   553\u2192\tfor _, c := range cmps {\n   554\u2192\t\tif !applyCompare(rv, c) {\n   555\u2192\t\t\treturn false\n   556\u2192\t\t}\n   557\u2192\t}\n   558\u2192\treturn true\n   559\u2192}\n   560\u2192\n   561\u2192// applyCompare applies the compare request.\n   562\u2192// If the comparison succeeds, it returns true. Otherwise, returns false.\n   563\u2192func applyCompare(rv mvcc.ReadView, c *pb.Compare) bool {\n   564\u2192\t// TODO: possible optimizations\n   565\u2192\t// * chunk reads for large ranges to conserve memory\n   566\u2192\t// * rewrite rules for common patterns:\n   567\u2192\t//\tex. \"[a, b) createrev > 0\" => \"limit 1 /\\ kvs > 0\"\n   568\u2192\t// * caching\n   569\u2192\trr, err := rv.Range(context.TODO(), c.Key, mkGteRange(c.RangeEnd), mvcc.RangeOptions{})\n   570\u2192\tif err != nil {\n   571\u2192\t\treturn false\n   572\u2192\t}\n   573\u2192\tif len(rr.KVs) == 0 {\n   574\u2192\t\tif c.Target == pb.Compare_VALUE {\n   575\u2192\t\t\t// Always fail if comparing a value on a key/keys that doesn't exist;\n   576\u2192\t\t\t// nil == empty string in grpc; no way to represent missing value\n   577\u2192\t\t\treturn false\n   578\u2192\t\t}\n   579\u2192\t\treturn compareKV(c, mvccpb.KeyValue{})\n   580\u2192\t}\n   581\u2192\tfor _, kv := range rr.KVs {\n   582\u2192\t\tif !compareKV(c, kv) {\n   583\u2192\t\t\treturn false\n   584\u2192\t\t}\n   585\u2192\t}\n   586\u2192\treturn true\n   587\u2192}\n   588\u2192\n   589\u2192func compareKV(c *pb.Compare, ckv mvccpb.KeyValue) bool {\n   590\u2192\tvar result int\n   591\u2192\trev := int64(0)\n   592\u2192\tswitch c.Target {\n   593\u2192\tcase pb.Compare_VALUE:\n   594\u2192\t\tv := []byte{}\n   595\u2192\t\tif tv, _ := c.TargetUnion.(*pb.Compare_Value); tv != nil {\n   596\u2192\t\t\tv = tv.Value\n   597\u2192\t\t}\n   598\u2192\t\tresult = bytes.Compare(ckv.Value, v)\n   599\u2192\tcase pb.Compare_CREATE:\n   600\u2192\t\tif tv, _ := c.TargetUnion.(*pb.Compare_CreateRevision); tv != nil {\n   601\u2192\t\t\trev = tv.CreateRevision\n   602\u2192\t\t}\n   603\u2192\t\tresult = compareInt64(ckv.CreateRevision, rev)\n   604\u2192\tcase pb.Compare_MOD:\n   605\u2192\t\tif tv, _ := c.TargetUnion.(*pb.Compare_ModRevision); tv != nil {\n   606\u2192\t\t\trev = tv.ModRevision\n   607\u2192\t\t}\n   608\u2192\t\tresult = compareInt64(ckv.ModRevision, rev)\n   609\u2192\tcase pb.Compare_VERSION:\n   610\u2192\t\tif tv, _ := c.TargetUnion.(*pb.Compare_Version); tv != nil {\n   611\u2192\t\t\trev = tv.Version\n   612\u2192\t\t}\n   613\u2192\t\tresult = compareInt64(ckv.Version, rev)\n   614\u2192\tcase pb.Compare_LEASE:\n   615\u2192\t\tif tv, _ := c.TargetUnion.(*pb.Compare_Lease); tv != nil {\n   616\u2192\t\t\trev = tv.Lease\n   617\u2192\t\t}\n   618\u2192\t\tresult = compareInt64(ckv.Lease, rev)\n   619\u2192\t}\n   620\u2192\tswitch c.Result {\n   621\u2192\tcase pb.Compare_EQUAL:\n   622\u2192\t\treturn result == 0\n   623\u2192\tcase pb.Compare_NOT_EQUAL:\n   624\u2192\t\treturn result != 0\n   625\u2192\tcase pb.Compare_GREATER:\n   626\u2192\t\treturn result > 0\n   627\u2192\tcase pb.Compare_LESS:\n   628\u2192\t\treturn result < 0\n   629\u2192\t}\n   630\u2192\treturn true\n   631\u2192}\n   632\u2192\n   633\u2192func (a *applierV3backend) applyTxn(ctx context.Context, txn mvcc.TxnWrite, rt *pb.TxnRequest, txnPath []bool, tresp *pb.TxnResponse) (txns int, err error) {\n   634\u2192\ttrace := traceutil.Get(ctx)\n   635\u2192\treqs := rt.Success\n   636\u2192\tif !txnPath[0] {\n   637\u2192\t\treqs = rt.Failure\n   638\u2192\t}\n   639\u2192\n   640\u2192\tfor i, req := 659\u2192\t\t\tresp, _, err := a.Put(ctx, txn, tv.RequestPut)\n   660\u2192\t\t\tif err != nil {\n   661\u2192\t\t\t\treturn 0, fmt.Errorf(\"applyTxn: failed Put: %w\", err)\n   662\u2192\t\t\t}\n *pb.TxnRequest, txnPath []bool, f checkReqFunc) (int, error) {\n  1042\u2192\ttxnCount := 0\n  1043\u2192\treqs := rt.Success\n  1044\u2192\tif !txnPath[0] {\n  1045\u2192\t\treqs = rt.Failure\n  1046\u2192\t}\n  1047\u2192\tfor _, req := range reqs {\n  1048\u2192\t\tif tv, ok := req.Request.(*pb.RequestOp_RequestTxn); ok && tv.RequestTxn != nil {\n  1049\u2192\t\t\ttxns, err := 1054\u2192\t\t\ttxnPath = txnPath[txns+1:]\n  1055\u2192\t\t\tcontinue\n  1056\u2192\t\t}\n  1057\u2192\t\tif err := f(rv, req); err != nil {\n  1058\u2192\t\t\treturn 0, err\n  1059\u2192\t\t}\n  1060\u2192\t}\n  1061\u2192\treturn txnCount, nil\n  1062\u2192}\n  1063\u2192\n  1064\u2192func (a *applierV3backend) checkRequestPut(rv mvcc.ReadView, reqOp *pb.RequestOp) error {\n  1065\u2192\ttv,
